Seventy-Year-Old Man Abducts Girl

Li Decheng Deceives Blind Woman

Jin Xiaozan Rescues Tu'er

Wu Xiufeng, a detective from the Municipal Police Bureau, was returning home from the team around 3 p.m. yesterday when he suddenly caught sight of an old man with a girl in a hurried manner while passing Keming Road. Upon closer inspection, the detective remembered that the old man had committed an abduction case in the Fifth District before, so he followed him. He saw the old man leading the girl to the door of 18 Shunda Lane and knocking on the door urgently, but no one answered. The old man then went to the back door. When he turned around, he noticed Detective Wu nearby and knew that something was wrong, so he abandoned the child and tried to escape, but was intercepted and brought back to the team with the girl. After a detailed interrogation by Captain Lu, the old man confessed his name as Li Decheng, aged seventy, from Qingjiang, currently living at 9 Xin Kaihe. He admitted to the abduction and confessed that he had seen a blind woman with a girl on a Jiangbei boat near Nanxing Bridge in Suzhou the previous month. He then had the intention to abduct the girl, so he spent time with the blind woman every day. The woman said that she was living in desperation and was about to starve to death, so I (the robber Li claimed) sent her a liter of rice and at the same time used a method to abduct the child. On the morning of July 21st of the lunar calendar, he took a car to Shanghai and sold her to the Chen Wei family in Shunda Lane for a price of eighty yuan. The Chen family only agreed to seventy yuan, so the deal was not settled. In total, he had sold three children to the Chen family, two of whom had already been resold. There was still one child that had not been sold. The abducted girl, named Jin Xiaozan, aged fourteen, from Funing, said that her mother had ordered her to go ashore to buy groceries when the boat docked at Nanxing Bridge in Suzhou around 8 p.m. the night before. She met the old man on Tanglu, who kept waving at her. She was unknowingly hypnotized and followed him to the station and took a car to Shanghai. Captain Lu obtained the confession and dispatched detectives Wu Zuorong and Yan Zhuming along with Detective Wu to Shunda Lane, where they arrested Chen Wei and rescued the abducted girl Tu'er. After interrogating the woman at the team, she confessed that she was fifty-two years old, from Fujian. The child Tu'er was sold to her by Li a few days ago for a price of 150 yuan. Her other statements were evasive. Captain Lu prepared a document based on the confession and sent the abductor Li Decheng and the child to the judicial section for processing. The woman Chen Wei was temporarily released on bail by her fellow villagers.

Scheme to Get Rich Quick Fooled

Two Gold Ingots Thrown into the Huangpu River

Where Did the Thousand Yuan in Banknotes Go?

No News of 200,000 in Unexpected Wealth

Such Things Actually Happen in the World

A certain person, A, who lives in Dongjiadu, South City, is a broker for a foreign company in the Public Concession. He goes out early and returns late, and he must pass through Xiaodongmen. One day in early this month, in the evening, A was returning home from work when a fortune teller, B, who had set up a stall inside a hotel in Xiaodongmen, suddenly shouted to A: "Sir, your luck is coming! You can get 200,000 in unexpected wealth within a few days!" A was temporarily bewildered and moved by this, so he entered his room and asked B about the method to get rich. B said: "I have a sandalwood Bodhisattva that is very efficacious. I can ask for it on your behalf." He immediately set up a table, burned incense, and after a while, B said that the Bodhisattva had already told him that you must prepare a five-tael gold ingot and throw it into the Huangpu River, and your fortune will arrive. He also said that this matter must not be told to others under any circumstances, otherwise, not only will you not get rich, but there will be misfortune. A believed this to be true and went home to raise money and exchange it for a five-tael gold ingot, which he sent to B. B took A to the Huangpu Bund, recited a few spells, and then threw the gold ingot into the river. Afterwards, they returned to the hotel, and B said to A that he would see wealth in three days. However, after three days passed, there was no news. A went to B's place again to inquire, and B again said that the Bodhisattva had said that you must throw another gold ingot into the river, and you will definitely get rich. A again went home to take the money and exchange it for a gold ingot, which he gave to B, and B did the same as before. (The gold ingots used twice were wrapped in white paper by B in the inn, and he secretly switched them.) A was still unaware and still believed it to be true. Unexpectedly, several days later, he still did not see any wealth. A went to B's place again to question him, and B said: "The wealth has arrived! You should quickly rent a house." A immediately went to Guangyuli, Nanyang Bridge, and rented a floor in a certain number. B then said to A: "You should quickly raise 2,000 yuan, and it will turn into 200,000." A said: "The money for the gold ingots was already pieced together, and it is really difficult to raise this huge sum now." B again said: "How can you miss such a good opportunity? If you don't have the full amount, you should raise 1,000 yuan, and I will also raise 1,000 yuan." A was still deluded and happily went home and pieced together the money. He also borrowed 1,000 yuan from friends and brought it to Guangyuli. B also prepared 1,000 yuan, all banknotes wrapped in paper into two packages. He set up a table, burned incense, and ordered A to kneel on the ground and kowtow. B took the opportunity to carry the money and flee. When A got up, B was gone. When he checked the two packages of banknotes, he found that they had turned into hell money. At this point, A finally realized that he had been fooled and regretted it, but it was too late.

Mei Fei Case to Be Sentenced

The Court Concluded the Interrogation Yesterday

Hu Yongquan Still Awaits Arrest

The case of the prostitute Mei Fei (also known as Chen Junxia) being accused by Tan Meiying, the wife of the guest Zhao Guangzu, of colluding with Hu Yongquan to defraud her of title deeds and other items has been repeatedly interrogated by the Special District Court. Hu has evaded arrest, and Mei Fei was ordered to pay a bail of 1,000 yuan. This has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Sun Yuan continued the trial. Hu Yongquan has not yet been arrested. The plaintiff's lawyer, Lu Qi, requested that the Mei Fei part be processed first. The court allowed it. Therefore, the plaintiff requested that the amount of Mei Fei's bail be increased because the four title deeds that were defrauded were more than 21 mu of land, with a value of more than 20,000, and a bail of 1,000 yuan was too light. Judge Sun then summoned Zhao Guangzu to testify about everything that happened after he met Hu Yongquan. Zhao repeated the entire story of how Mei Fei introduced him to Hu Yongquan and how he entrusted Hu to buy a car. According to Mei Fei, she met Zhao Guangzu through a guest surnamed Gu in May or June of last year. Zhao visited her twice, then came to her place for tea. Zhao said that he was studying at Guanghua University and had never married. He wanted to marry her and said that his property rights were still managed by others on his behalf, and he asked her to forgive him for this after the marriage. Near the end of the year, Zhao asked her to withdraw from the brothel and rent a house to live together. At this time, he said that his property rights were managed by his sister on his behalf, and he said that she would belong to him when she got married. She believed his words and went into debt to make a living, owing more than 2,000 yuan. As for Hu Yongquan, she met him at the mahjong table. The meeting between Hu and Zhao was not introduced by her, and she did not give Zhao's title deeds to her. Judge Sun pointed out that Zhao had testified that the title deeds were handed over to Mei Fei to be transferred to Hu, but Mei Fei denied it. Therefore, he asked Zhao if he had any evidence in this regard. Zhao said that they had a deep emotional connection at the time and that they had directly handed them over, and there was no evidence and no third party was present. Judge Sun then threw two letters from Zhao to Mei Fei submitted by the defendant's lawyer to Zhao to read. After Zhao read them, he denied that the letters were written by him and requested a handwriting analysis. He then wrote (Chen Junxia, Yulin Lane, Guling Road) and other words in court as instructed by the judge. The lawyers on both sides debated each other, and the court announced that the verdict would be announced next Tuesday. Hu Yongquan's part will be heard separately after he is arrested.

Old Murder Case Reopened

The Wife of a Military Officer Died Tragically Five Years Ago

Zhang Gu's Mother and Son Accused of Murder

Zhao Zhang, the sister of Zhang Jinfu from Yancheng, married Zhao Fengrong, who held the position of battalion commander during the warlord era. In 1924, during the Qilu War, Zhao was a frontline military officer on the Qilu side and died in the battle of Liuhe. At that time, Zhao Zhang was still a young woman living in a dream. When the bad news came, she was grief-stricken, but she also received a pension. Zhang Gu, a concubine of Zhang Xuhua, a quartermaster in Zhao's battalion, was Zhao Zhang's godmother. She brought Zhao Zhang to Shanghai to return the remains of her deceased husband. On May 7th of the lunar calendar in 1925, Zhao Zhang's body was suddenly discovered at the Wangjiazhai in Gaolang Bridge, not far from her residence. At that time, the former Prosecutor's Office verified the identity and collected the body and investigated the murder. At that time, the Fourth Precinct of the Fifth District received an anonymous letter alleging that Zhang Gu had a major suspicion. When the body was verified, Zhang Gu showed recognition, and the police station also investigated, but there was no evidence to support it, so they did not pursue it. Last month, Zhang Jinfu went to the Yangshupu Police Station to accuse Zhang Gu and her son Zhang Wanchang of murdering his sister. They were immediately arrested and sent to the Special District Court. Because the case was originally a mainland case, it was transferred to the local court for investigation yesterday.

Public Opposition to Takashashi Sandbar Project: Foreign Company Building Oil Tanks

The German-owned "Deutche Vacuum Oel Actien Gesellschaft" (德士古, known as "Texas Company" in Chinese transliteration) has been attempting to purchase land from residents on Takashashi Sandbar (高橋沙) to construct oil tanks for storing dangerous goods. This has been repeatedly opposed by the local residents. The matter has not yet been resolved, but the foreign company has now hired laborers to begin construction in recent days, leading to strong opposition from the sandbar residents. Yesterday, two to three hundred people, including local public organizations and sandbar residents, held a meeting on the sandbar. After discussion, they put forward five reasons: (1) The Texas Company is encroaching into the interior, violating the trade treaty. (2) The company is violating the Takashashi Sandbar land regulations of the Ministry of Finance. (3) It is violating the regulations for building oil tanks. (4) It has not submitted an application for approval to the government but has forcibly started construction. (5) It is violating local public opinion by forcibly acquiring land from the people and cutting off the livelihoods of farmers. Based on the above reasons, they should immediately petition the municipal government to confiscate the sandbar land that the Texas Company forcibly purchased against public opinion, in order to maintain the rule of law and serve as a warning to others.

Hunan Rice Not Yet Shipped to Shanghai in Large Quantities

It is now the Autumn Equinox, and the early rice harvest in various villages has been gradually completed. New early rice from both the northern and southern rice markets in this city has also been successively arriving on the market. However, rice prices remain firm and have not fallen. According to rice merchants yesterday, the reason is that the amount of new early rice arriving is small. Although Hunan has had a bumper harvest this year, the rice from farmers there is fully stored and piled up like mountains, making it impossible to transport it out of the province. Therefore, those in the rice industry in this city who go to purchase it have not yet shipped it to Shanghai in large quantities, so the market price remains high. However, with the assurance of a bumper harvest in various villages this year, it is expected that in about a month or so, large quantities of new early rice will arrive on the market from various villages. At that time, it is hoped that rice prices will fall.

Electrical Company: Revised Procedures for Notifying Customers of Changes to Electrical Equipment

To ensure safety, the Electrical Company (電氣公司) requires that all customer-installed electrical equipment pass inspection before a meter is installed and power is connected. This procedure is specified in its operational regulations as follows: "The company will send personnel to inspect within five days from the date of receiving the application form, power supply contract, and deposit. If it is considered qualified, the meter will be installed and power connected. Otherwise, the company will fill out a modification notice indicating the points that need to be modified, which the customer will forward to the electrical materials store or electrical contractor for modification within a specified period. After the modification, another notification will be sent for re-inspection..." Previously, the Water and Electricity Association believed that having the customer forward the modification notice caused delays and that it would be better for the company to directly deliver it to the contractor to save time. They petitioned the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to correct this. The bureau considered it feasible and ordered each company to amend the inspection clause in its business regulations accordingly. It is now known that each company has complied and changed it to "(...the company will fill out a modification notice...)". This has also been reported by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to the Municipal Government for record.

Shaohsing Native Place Association: Seeking a Youth Who Has Become Disillusioned With Life

According to Hu Huan-ran (胡煥然) from Shangyu (上虞), the Shaohsing Native Place Association (紹興旅滬同鄉會) reports that his brother, Zan-ran (贊然), 18 years old, wearing a white Zhongshan suit, Western-style hair, and leather shoes, came to Shanghai from his hometown on the 10th of this month. A few days later, his family received a letter from him stating that he was coughing up blood after arriving in Shanghai and had decided to commit suicide due to his pessimistic thoughts. The letter did not mention where he intended to commit suicide. His whereabouts are unknown. It is hoped that anyone who knows his whereabouts will report to the association. His family will offer a substantial reward.

Municipal Government: Banning Private Cemeteries From Simultaneously Establishing Funeral Homes

There are quite a few funeral homes (丙舍) in this city. The issue of dealing with existing temporary coffins has already become difficult. Recently, the Municipal Health Bureau discovered that some private cemeteries are also simultaneously establishing funeral homes. The bureau believes that this has a significant impact on dealing with the issue of temporary coffins. To reduce difficulties and facilitate management, they have petitioned the municipal government to prohibit all private cemeteries from simultaneously establishing funeral homes. After receiving the petition, the municipal government stated that the nature of cemeteries is to provide a permanent solution for the disposal of coffins. Simultaneously establishing funeral homes undermines the purpose of establishing cemeteries and is inconsistent with cemetery regulations. Therefore, it should be banned. Yesterday, they specifically instructed the bureau that private cemeteries should not be allowed to simultaneously establish funeral homes in the future. The bureau was also instructed to investigate in detail how many private cemeteries in this city have already established funeral homes and submit a report for review in order to comply with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry and ban them accordingly.

Rice Shop Partner Bankrupted, Family Ruined

Fortunately, the shop owner showed compassion.

The lost money will not be pursued.

Bao Ming-sheng (鮑明生) from Chuansha (川沙) was a partner in a rice shop in Zhoupu (周浦), Pudong. Last month, when the new rice from Pudong came on the market, the shop's daily sales of new brown rice were substantial. Bao was assigned by the shop to be stationed in Shanghai as a salesman to transport the rice to Shanghai for milling. In the middle of last month, Bao received 1,200 yuan in cash in Zhabei and took it back to Zhoupu. When he was about to hand the money over to the accountant in the shop, he was surprised to find that the money was no longer in his bag. Bao searched everywhere in a panic, but to no avail. The shop refused to take responsibility because the amount of money lost was too large, so they demanded compensation from Bao's introducer. The introducer interceded with the shop, suggesting that Bao and the shop each bear half of the loss. Bao immediately paid 300 yuan, and the remaining half was to be deducted from his salary in installments. Bao was unable to borrow money from relatives and friends and had to sell his ancestral farmland, which was still not enough. Bao's wife argued with him when he sold the land. Bao had been looking haggard and often sighing since he lost the shop's money, and the shop had assigned his sales position to another partner. Bao thought that the shop considered him useless, so he had been restless lately. A few days ago, he was sent to the countryside to collect goods. Bao took the opportunity to return home, but his wife's relatives ridiculed him for going bankrupt. Upon hearing this, he became very angry and swallowed red-headed matches and attempted suicide. People discovered this and sent him to the hospital for treatment. When Bao arrived home and learned of this, he fainted immediately. Bao's mother saw this and shouted, also fainting to the ground. Although she was awakened, Bao's mother's health was poor, and medical treatment was ineffective. She died the day before yesterday. Bao suddenly developed a mental illness. Bao's wife is still in the hospital. After Bao's mother died, relatives purchased a coffin and held a funeral. Bao's shop owner, upon hearing that Bao had ruined his family and harmed himself, felt very compassionate and did not want Bao to pay back the lost money. He sent someone to return the 300 yuan that Bao had already paid to the shop to Bao and told him to rest and recover. Bao's relatives sent a letter of thanks and it was heard that Bao's relatives plan to send Bao to the Shanghai New Puyu Hall (新普育堂) for medical treatment so that he can recover quickly and return to normal.

Detention of Workers Involved in a Brawl

Yang Bin-fa (楊彬發) and others, carpenters residing in the Hung-mu Gang (紅木帮) of Huining Road (徽寗路) in the Southern City (南巿), were involved in an incident. Chen Jin-fa (陳金發), an apprentice dyer at the Tong-de Silk Weaving Factory (同德絲光廠), bumped into Yang Bin-fa due to an eye ailment. Yang then hit Chen, and Chen Jin-fa fled into the factory. They arranged to meet at the Puyu Road (普育路) teahouse within the jurisdiction of the Second Precinct, Second Division (二區二分所) at 7 or 8 a.m. yesterday (the 18th). Yang Bin-fa invited forty to fifty people, and the dyeing gang also gathered about seventy or eighty people. Each held iron and wooden sticks, creating a very menacing atmosphere, as if facing a major enemy. Seeing that the dyeing gang had more people, Yang Bin-fa feared that they would not be able to withstand the attack and reported to Chief Guo (郭) of the Second Precinct, Second Division. Chief Guo, upon hearing the report, stated that the group dared to gather a crowd, carry weapons, and engage in a brawl based on a grudge, which was completely illegal and undisciplined. He immediately dispatched Patrol Officer Jin (金) with police officers to suppress and arrest them. By the time they arrived, the gangs were already fighting. Under the command of Patrol Officer Jin, the police officers bravely arrested them. However, since the members of the gangs were all muscular and strong, it was very difficult to catch them. As a result, six members of the Hung-mu Gang, including Yang Bin-fa, and four members of the dyeing gang, including Ding Qi-yi (丁七一), were arrested. Zou Yi-yuan (鄒義元) of the Hung-mu Gang suffered a head injury, and Chen Guo-qian (陳國千) of the dyeing gang suffered a head injury. Five wooden sticks and one iron stick were also seized as weapons. All were taken to the station. After questioning by Chief Guo, it was determined that Yang Bin-fa and others had gathered a crowd to brawl, resulting in injuries to both sides. The case was considered criminal, and Yang Bin-fa, Zou Yi-yuan, Zeng Li-sheng (曾禮生), Zhou Mao-sheng (周茂生), Lei Sheng-fa (雷勝發), Zeng Rui-lin (曾瑞林), Ding Qi-yi, Chen Guo-qian, Sun Fu-chang (孫福昌), and Wang A-ao (王阿鰲), a total of ten people, along with the evidence, were sent to the local court for investigation.

Pedicab Crushes a Person to Death

At 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon, Wang Si-tong (王思統), a Northerner aged 27 who worked at the Public Security Bureau, was driving a motorized pedicab on the Jing'an Temple Road (靜安寺路) in West Shanghai. Two people were riding with him. He accidentally lost control and the pedicab overturned, crushing Wang's abdomen. He was barely breathing. West Detective No. 147 from the Xinzha Police Station (新閘捕房) arrived, hired a car, and sent him to Renji Hospital (仁濟醫院) for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died at around 10:00 PM last night. His friend, Chang Juan-qiu (常娟球), 27 years old, also suffered skin abrasions on his hands and feet. After examination by a doctor, he was found to be unharmed.

Pedicab Driver Hangs Himself

Zhang Da-xiang (張大向), a pedicab driver from Tongzhou (通州) residing at No. 81 Zhangjiabang (張家浜), Qiqihar Road (齊齊哈爾路), West Shanghai, was 40 years old. Due to the rising cost of living and his meager income, which was insufficient to cover expenses, he became disillusioned with life. He took advantage of a moment when no one was watching and hanged himself the night before last. The person living with him discovered it, but it was too late to save him. He immediately reported it to the police station in charge, which reported it to the local court. Yesterday afternoon, the prosecutor was dispatched to the scene to confirm that he had died by hanging. They ordered the preparation of a coffin and burial.

Monk Commits Sodomy on Young Apprentice

Chen A-liu (陳阿六年), 31 years old from Tongzhou (通州), runs a pastry shop at No. 56 Tangfang Alley (糖坊衖) outside the Little South Gate (小南門). Liu Lao-er (劉老二), who lives at No. 70 in the same alley, owed him more than 1,000 cash. After repeatedly demanding payment without success, he sent his 13-year-old apprentice, Zheng He-hou (鄭和厚), to demand payment at around 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. It happened that Liu was out, and Miao Wang (妙旺), a 24-year-old monk from Anhui who had been a monk since childhood, a companion of a monk named Jie San (戒三), was waiting for him in the parlor. Since he had not met Jie San, he sat and waited. At that time, the apprentice Zheng He-hou was about to leave because Liu was not there. Unexpectedly, the monk Miao Wang saw that Zheng had a pleasing appearance, much like a girl. He was immediately filled with lust and had evil thoughts. He forcibly dragged Zheng upstairs into the bedroom, pressed him down on the bed, took off his pants, and committed sodomy. The apprentice Zheng was in unbearable pain and cried out loudly, but his mouth was covered to prevent him from making a sound, and he was further threatened. Because Zheng was weak and unable to resist, he was violated. Afterwards, he felt inflammation and pain in his anus. He pulled up his pants and staggered out, tearfully recounting everything to his master. When Chen heard about this, he was furious and immediately rushed over, but the monk Miao Wang had already fled. Although he searched for him in vain, he could not find him. At around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, he encountered him on the road and immediately grabbed him and called out to Police Officer Miao Dian-ke (苗殿科) of the 26th post, who brought him back to the First Precinct, Third Division (一區三分所) under the charge of Chief Jin (金). After a preliminary interrogation, he ordered a document to be prepared and transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for investigation.

Coolie Commits Suicide by Drowning

At around 8:00 AM yesterday morning, a coolie, about 50 years old, committed suicide by jumping into the river from the Bird Town Road Bridge (鳥鎭路橋) in Zhabei. He drowned before he could be rescued. His body was recovered by the boatmen of the Life Saving Bureau. He was wearing black clothes, with bare head and bare feet.

Unidentified Male Body Recovered from Xinzha Bridge River

Yesterday, the patrol boat of the Life Saving Bureau recovered the body of an unidentified male from the Xinzha Bridge River (新閘橋河) in Zhabei. He was about 50 years old, wearing a Yuan cloth lined jacket and blue cloth shirt and trousers. There was a two-inch wide knife wound on his forehead, but it was not very deep. There were also minor injuries on his hands. The water patrol team ordered the local guarantor, Shen Xiao-he (沈小和), to report to the local court for inspection.

Thugs Violently Beat Boatmen

The Problem of Docking at the Yitai Pier (義泰碼頭) in Pudong

The Evil Bullying and Strange Behavior of Ruffians

At around 12:00 PM yesterday morning, three people, each carrying serious injuries, reported to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau Water Patrol Team (上海巿公安局水巡隊), claiming that Chen Guang-gao (陳廣高), Liu Xu-yun (劉旭雲), and Xu De-cai (徐得財) were all boatmen from Jiangbei (江北) who made a living by sailing barges. This morning, when they docked their boats near the Yitai Pier (義泰碼頭) in Bailianjing (白蓮涇), a boat came to force its way into the dock and squeezed them out. When they protested slightly, they were gathered and attacked by a dozen or so people, each carrying iron rulers, wooden sticks, and other weapons, causing them to be weak and unable to resist, suffering injuries all over their bodies. They requested that the matter be investigated. When the police were dispatched to investigate and arrest the perpetrators, they had all dispersed. Only Gao Er-lang (高二郞), a boatman from Chongming (崇明), was apprehended. The team was instructed to prepare a document explaining the incident and submit it to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for investigation. Subsequently, it was heard that the Bailianjing Police Station (白蓮涇派出所) of the Third Team of the same patrol team also had a boatman with a head injury bleeding profusely, claiming that Wu Ji-lang (吳基郞), 30 years old from Chongming, made a living by boating. This morning, when he docked his boat next to the Yitai Pier to prepare to load coal, three Jiangbei barge boats rushed over and forced him to move his boat. Because he refused, he was attacked by a crowd of people who beat him and struck his head with an axe, causing him to be injured and bleed. He requested a thorough investigation. The police station dispatched police officers to investigate and arrest the perpetrators. The ringleaders were nowhere to be found. Only Hao Ji-lin (郝紀林), Liu Chang-fu (劉長福), Chen Ming-guo (陳明國), and other boatmen from the three boats were arrested, along with the axes and other weapons. They were brought back and transferred to the Southern City General Team. They then prepared a document explaining the incident and submitted it to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Cargo Ship Collides, Killing a Girl

The Beikou (北口) sandboat Jin Zeng-li (金增利) was fully loaded with bamboo, kiln goods, etc., and was sailing to Yingkou. It was docked at the southern end of the Jiu Ji Pier (久記碼頭) in the Southern City. Yesterday, it was preparing to set sail and hire a police boat to leave the harbor. However, when the Jin ship turned around to release the mooring ropes, it ...

Page 12

happened that the Jiangbei (江北) boat Jiang Zhong-he (蔣仲和), carrying Rongji (榮記) foreign goods and candy, was heading to Minhang. Seeing that the tugboat was traveling at full speed, it was trying to avoid it, but it was too late. It was struck by the stern of the Jin ship. The load of the Jiang ship was very heavy. After being hit, the bow of the ship broke off and gradually sank. Fortunately, nearby boats on the Pudong beach saw this and tried their best to help, dragging the Jiang ship to the beach and stranding it. When the collision occurred, Jiang's wife was holding a girl and sitting on the stern of the ship, sewing clothes. She was knocked into the river. She was rescued by a neighboring boat, but the girl was not rescued. Jiang is now negotiating with the Jin ship for compensation for the loss. It is heard that the candy on the ship was insured against water damage.

County Government Prevents Bandits From Fleeing Into the Territory

Xiong Shihui (熊式輝), Commander-in-Chief for the Suppression of Bandits in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, has learned that the bandit leader Tai Bao A Shu (太保阿書) has fled back to Jinshan to loot. He has appointed Hu Zhengji (胡正濟) as the temporary commander for bandit suppression in Jinshan, Fengxian, Qingpu, and Pinghu counties, with a deadline to clear them out by the end of September. It is known that Tai Bao A Shu's bandit gang still has three to four hundred people. Although they have been attacked by land and naval forces and police after looting Jinshan, their strength has not been dispersed. They are currently hiding in Gao Xu (高墟), which is located at the border of Qingpu and Wujiang. The Shanghai County Government has received successive telegrams from the Bandit Suppression Department of the Three Provinces and the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department, ordering the county to launch a major suppression campaign in the coming days. If the bandits flee into the territory, the county police should assist in the operation to eliminate any future problems. County Magistrate Yan Zuo (嚴縣長作) has ordered the County Public Security Bureau (縣公安局) to instruct all sub-bureaus bordering neighboring counties to comply and report the bandits' situation at any time.

County Public Security Bureau Chief Going to Province for Promotion

Shen Jing-hua (沈靖華), Chief of the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau, took a train to the province last night to visit the Civil Affairs Director to report on all bureau affairs. Chief Clerk Cai Zhong-ji (蔡鍾驥) is temporarily acting in his place. It is heard that he will return to Shanghai in two or three days.

The Grand Scene of Last Night's Bicycle Race

Zheng Long-fei Wins the Three-Nation Race

The third cycle of competitions held at the Weile Garden (衛樂園) on Haig Road (海格路) last night from 9:00 pm featured twelve different events. After each race, there was a motorcycle performance, which was very exciting and exhilarating. The five-lap motorcycle contest between Allen and Ye Sheng (葉聲) in the fourth event drew a lot of applause. The China-Japan-Annam (Vietnam) three-nation race in the fifth event was particularly eye-catching. Each country sent two of their best riders. China sent Zheng Long-fei (鄭龍飛) and Gao Yong-nian (高永年). After ten laps of fierce fighting, Zheng Long-fei of China won the championship. Zheng's driving skills were as agile as a dragon flying or a swallow soaring, so his name Long-fei (龍飛) can be said to be truly fitting. The leading car race in the sixth event was also one of the highlights of last night. In the end, the victory also went to Zhu Liang (朱良), a Chinese athlete.

Dentist Sun Xia-min is Skilled in Teeth Cleaning

Dentist Sun Xia-min (孫夏民) at No. 9 Park Road (派克路) and Baker Road (白克路) is well-versed in dental medicine, including tooth extraction, filling, and repair. He is especially skilled in teeth cleaning. Any yellow or black stains can be removed through his treatment, resulting in a bright, clean, and beautiful appearance. This is the only good way to prevent dental problems. Dentist Sun has reduced his fees to promote oral hygiene, so many people have been going to him for teeth cleaning lately.

Dr. Liu Practices Law

After returning from his studies, Dr. Liu (劉君之謀), a Doctor of Law from the University of Leuven in Belgium, served as the Director of the Hankou Local Office. After completing his term, he was hired by the Central University as a law professor. Dr. Liu has profound legal knowledge. He has now established an office at No. 2 Baker Road in this city to practice law. Liu is determined to handle everything himself and will conduct all civil and criminal cases in accordance with the law.

"Anti-Drug Monthly" Published

The "Anti-Drug Monthly" (拒毒月刋) is a periodical published by the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association (中華國民拒毒會). It has been published for nearly four years and is approaching its fortieth issue. People from all over the world who are concerned about the anti-drug issue and China's opium ban regularly subscribe to the publication. In addition to publishing information about the anti-drug movement and opium ban news, the content also includes contributions from various sectors and speeches from celebrities. It is heard that the recent issue No. 39 was published yesterday.

Lost Boy Waiting to be Claimed

Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Fourth District sent a lost boy named Rong Hong-zhen (榮洪珍). According to him, he is eight years old. His parents are Rong Zhao-ji (榮兆基), who sells soybean oil. He does not know the address of his home. He said he went to the suburbs to catch crickets but forgot the way home. The child has a flat head, long face, and a large scar near his left ear. He is wearing a fine blue striped Fu silk jacket and white checkered ramie gauze trousers, barefoot without shoes or socks. He has been sent to the New Jin Yu Tang (新晋育堂) to be cared for while waiting to be claimed.

Wende Lane Residents Association Established

The houses in Wende Lane (文德里) on Yangshupu Road (楊樹浦路) have been built for more than ten years and have never been repaired, resulting in disrepair. The houses are not adjacent to any roads, and the access roads are not owned by the homeowners. The land is extremely low-lying, and it is muddy when it rains. Heavy rains turn the area into a swamp. Therefore, the residents are mostly hardworking workers from nearby factories. The rent has been increased three times over the years. Originally, Xu Wen-ji (徐文記) collected the rent, but recently it has been changed to Wufengchangji Zhuang (五豐昌記莊). Last month, Zhuang made some minor repairs to the outside of the houses and raised the rent for the fourth time, from 7.5 yuan per building to 11 yuan. The residents were shocked and unanimously refused to accept the rent increase, leading to a dispute. The residents then initiated the organization of a tenants' association to deal with the situation. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the initiators convened a meeting of all the tenants to discuss how to proceed. More than eighty tenants attended the meeting. The meeting was opened with a bell, followed by ceremonial procedures. Wu De-xiang (吳德祥) was elected as chairman, and Gu Feng-qi (顧峰奇) as recorder. The chairman first reported the purpose of the meeting and the significance of organizing the tenants' association. Then, the tenants unanimously stated that the rent has been increased three times in recent years, and this time the increase is almost half of the total amount. In this time of expensive rice and firewood and difficult living conditions, they cannot afford such a burden. They absolutely do not agree with the rent increase. It was resolved that (1) a tenants' association would be actively organized; (2) Jiang Jun (蔣俊), Shen Xin-you (沈新友), Sun Li-yao (孫笠卿), Guo Zheng-qi (郭政啟), Shao Yu-cheng (邵玉成), Wu De-xiang, Tian Bao-zhu (田寶珠), Xu Ru-ming (許如明), Liu Sheng-pei (劉生培), Chen Chang-fu (陳長富), Zhou Yuan-kui (周願奎) and eleven others were elected as preparation committee members; (3) funding would be temporarily sought by the initiators, and the funds would be repaid when membership fees are collected in the future; (4) rent would not be paid temporarily until the landlord clearly stated that they would not raise the rent; (5) Gu Feng-qi would be the honorary secretary. The meeting adjourned, and it was already five o'clock.

Free Talk

A Word or Two

— Long

No matter what the matter, if one aspect is disappointing, another aspect is bound to be satisfying. This is true of major events like wars and minor events like divorces.

Cars are indeed faster than walking, but cars are prone to accidents, often resulting in tragedies of self-injury and injury to others. Therefore, the ancients had the saying "contentment with walking as if riding in a carriage."

The more vibrant and dazzling the flower, the newer and more spoiled the youth.

Today's wealthy are far less free to come and go than the poor, and they are always worried about things. Those who hold great power and enjoy great fame also have the lament of "I cannot proceed, brother."

At least one or two people are unhappy and jealous when a free marriage is held in a church.

Old scholars have more stubbornness than the ability to do evil, while good young people have the heart to love their country but lack the power to kill the enemy.

Before one becomes addicted to opium, one hates opium smokers like enemies. Once one becomes addicted, one wishes that everyone else would join in.

Women's hearts turn outwards, so the sons born of women are good at blaming others and bad at blaming themselves.

Promoting universal education is easier and more effective than high-sounding plans to save the country, because illiterate compatriots have no understanding of the meaning of "overturned nest."

The influx of foreign goods is a sign of gradual national invasion, while the development of domestic products is a sign of national strength.

Model Military Man Luo Xiankai

— Fang Er

For the past ten days, fellow Hunanese in Beijing have been telling each other in astonishment about Luo Xiankai, the model military man, in connection with the recent communist unrest in Changsha.

Luo Xiankai was from the eastern countryside of Changsha. As a child, he was poor and herded pigs and cattle. Occasionally dissatisfied with his master, he would angrily beg for food in all directions. Later, he joined the army as a camp follower. After a long time, he became a soldier and eventually rose to the rank of brigade commander through merit. He had been in the military for nearly forty years, moving and fighting in battles. He often spoke to people with relish about his experiences and said that he had nothing when he started and that he was content with his current status. People admired him for this. When he was a brigade commander, the Hunan authorities were considering reducing the size of the army. He was the first to request retirement to his hometown, setting an example for the other generals. Public opinion called him a model military man, mainly because he only reached the rank of brigade commander and had less than a million in assets. He retired when he thought he was rich and noble enough, which is rare among modern military men.

He built a villa in the middle of the Xiang River on the Shui Lu Zhou (Water and Land Island) west of Changsha. He spent the summer there to escape the heat and returned to his hometown in the winter. He often carried money into the city alone and brought goods home. Dressed in coarse clothes and cloth shoes, he looked like a country elder. Cart drivers and boatmen who knew he was Brigade Commander Luo competed to be hired by him, hoping to receive dozens or hundreds of cash as a reward.

Although he was sixty or seventy years old, he looked like he was in his fifties. Because he was a veteran general from Hunan and was old, fellow military officers from the same hometown, including Cheng Qian and Zhao Hengti, all respectfully called him "Elder Ding." His courtesy name was Ding'an, just as the Beiyang military men called Duan Zhiqian "Elder Zhi." Even his old superior, Tan Weigong, treated him with great respect.

After his retirement, although the Hunan authorities did not give him any military posts, they still entrusted him with the positions of director of the Changsha militia and director-general of the Hunan Province Clearance Office from the Zhao Hengti era onwards. Hunan militia forces, from Zeng Guofan until now, are known for their indiscriminate killings. Each county has countless militia sub-bureaus, which are countless killing machines. Provincial and county general bureaus and local authorities cannot control them and simply ignore them. They are relied upon to suppress bandits. Since the suppression of the communists, the Hunan militia has killed countless people. This time, when the communists entered Changsha, they were satisfied to get Luo Xiankai, the director-general of the militia. Alas, the communists' means of revenge were truly cruel.

A Record of Shandong Provincial Gold Coins

— Dingsheng

China's monetary system has reached the extreme of disorder. Since the late Qing dynasty, those who have discussed the monetary system have known that only the adoption of the gold standard could compete with the world. However, this has never been implemented due to the lack of gold production and the emptiness of the national treasury. However, local authorities in various provinces have occasionally independently raised funds to mint provincial gold coins. People only know that Tang Jiyao minted Yunnan provincial gold coins after the success of the National Protection War, but they do not know that Zhang Zongchang of Shandong also minted gold coins in the Republic of China Year 15. This is something that those who study currency should know. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Zhang Zongchang had seized both the Yan and Lu provinces, so the Tianjin General Mint, the largest mint in China, also belonged to Zhang. This mint was founded by Li Hongzhang during his tenure as Governor-General of Zhili and had complete facilities. It could mint two million silver coins and three million copper subsidiary coins per day. Zhang then recommended Li Houzuo and Ren Yuan'dao as supervisors and directors. Li and Ren were very keen on reforming the monetary system and proposed to mint gold coins using the gold from Shandong.

The Shandong peninsula is rich in gold, but unfortunately, the mining methods have not been improved and people pay little attention to it. According to the Shandong Provincial Gold Coin Plan compiled by Li and Ren, if the Shandong gold mines were subsidized and reorganized by the provincial government, they could produce one million taels of gold per year. This would allow for the minting of four million ten-yuan gold coins per year. Before the gold standard was established, merchants would accept the coins at market prices and the government and people would benefit. Zhang urged them to proceed and ordered the initial minting of ten-yuan and twenty-yuan coins. Li and Ren then planned carefully, hired Yang Zijia, a graduate of a French university, and Li Zuxun, a German chemistry PhD. Italian engravers were hired to meticulously manufacture steel dies, which took months to complete. Their design was even more beautiful than British and American gold coins. The reverse side featured a fire dragon and the twelve symbols of imperial authority, while the obverse side featured ears of grain and the words "Shandong Provincial Gold Coin, Republic of China Year 15." Zhang was very pleased with this and ordered the minting to begin. The first batch of 200,000 coins were minted, and people rushed to collect them, but few circulated in the market. When the National Revolutionary Army marched out of the Yangtze River, Ren went to Hankou and Li resigned due to illness. The matter then ended. This matter was very short-lived and few coins were minted. Recently, they have been bought up by people from the east and are almost exhausted. Few people know about it. I am writing this to provide a page for the history of the Chinese monetary system.

The Principal Swallowing Pears

— Guqu Yunji

Autumn is deep, and the students are returning to school with their book bags. This is a commonplace event and not worth mentioning in detail. However, I recently heard a story about a pear-swallowing incident at a certain girls' school, which was tortuous, humorous, and thought-provoking. Therefore, I casually record it to make my point.

Soliciting a Letter: There is a girl here who is graceful and considers herself a good scholar. She boldly sent a letter to someone expressing her feelings. This girl has always been unwilling to be in debt to others. Thus, there are many troubles in the Central Plains.

Gifting Pears: A certain young man is closest to the girl. Their correspondence is also the most frequent, with almost two letters a day. Recently, he returned from Tianjin and brought back more than ten Dalia pears, which he sent to the girl. The girl was out, so the principal obtained the pears and a love letter. The letter was commonplace, so the principal did not intend to investigate. However, the principal was from the north and knew that these pears were not easy to obtain, so he thought of a way to deal with them.

Swallowing the Pears: The principal took the pears and the letter back to her office, summoned the girl and questioned her. The girl swore that there was nothing between them, so the principal did not investigate. Although the girl knew that the pears were valuable, she did not dare to mention them because the principal had not mentioned them either. Thus, the principal and her close staff were able to enjoy the taste of their hometown to the full.

Epilogue: A certain person on the staff ate her fill and smiled as she told people about it. The girl thought about it and was dissatisfied. She resolutely went to ask the principal, intending to ask for the gift back. The principal gave a jumbled response and told her to discuss it later and that she would definitely find a way to compensate her. The girl retreated, but I don't know if this person from the south will be able to vomit out something true from the fake.

The Flavors of Autumn: More at Huishan

— Jing Mengdie

A trip to Huishan in Wuxi is more rewarding in the autumn than in the spring. Spring outings are only for visual pleasure, while autumn outings can also satisfy the palate. Recently, as the west wind rises, a refreshing atmosphere greets people, and the mountain's fine fruits are available in season. The most common are the four-cornered water caltrop and the osmanthus chestnut. They are sold everywhere. Guests who climb the Zhulu Mountain Villa can enjoy the four-cornered water caltrop with Two Springs tea, which can be said to be a particularly flavorful experience. This water caltrop is produced in the nearby Sunxiang and Da Xuankou areas. Whenever it is time to pick the water caltrop, you can see girls on the lake in a small wooden basin, gazing over the vast expanse of water. Their misty hair emerges from the shimmering water, captivating and astounding people. These girls navigate the dangerous waters with ease and grace. This is a remarkable scene and an extraordinary skill. However, because the output is large, the quality is good and the price is low, less than two hundred cash per catty. Osmanthus chestnuts are very precious and expensive. Distant visitors buy them and give them to relatives and friends as a valuable gift. The price is one silver dollar for two catties. In fact, according to the people of Wuxi, the only true Huishan chestnuts that are of the osmanthus variety and contain the taste of osmanthus are the five trees in front of the Niangniang Hall (an ancient temple). The rest are merely imitations and should only be called Huishan chestnuts, not osmanthus chestnuts. Towards the end of autumn, when the chestnuts in the mountains are almost gone, residents secretly bring in goods from other places and mix them in to profit. At that time, even Huishan chestnuts cannot be obtained. I say that there are few things in the world where name and reality match. Most people are simply eating what they hear and can rarely discern the taste. So don't blame them for being deceived.

A Record of Golden Needles Saving the World

— Yifen

The golden needle is the oldest form of medicine in our country. Mr. Huang Shiping, a national doctor in the late Qing Dynasty, was famous for it, and my friend Mr. Fang Shenyu inherited his teachings. Shenyu once held a military command in Henan in his youth, but he left due to frustration and devoted himself to the study of medicine. All kinds of difficult and complicated diseases, both internal and external, were cured by his hands. After arriving in Shanghai, his reputation spread rapidly. A few years ago, a woman surnamed Qu from Guangdong had a growth in her abdomen. Shenyu cured it with needles. A wealthy overseas Chinese merchant surnamed Yuan suffered from stiff neck and back, and after visiting famous doctors in Germany and France without success, he heard of Shenyu's name and returned to China to show it to him. He was cured in forty-five days. His skills can be called miraculous. He is amiable and chivalrous, and he treats the diseases of others as if they were his own. Even if the poor come to him for treatment, he inquires attentively and does not care about money. He is unlike the famous doctors of today. Friends and relatives who come to him for help are always readily accommodated. He is dedicated to friendship and righteousness, even in the cold of winter and the heat of summer. He also founded the Yixue Huilian Society and published four kinds of books, all valuable medical works that benefit the world. Mr. Chu Lantang De Yi gave him a couplet: "The famous words of Jiushi are verified in the Lu's Spring and Autumn Annals, the divine techniques of needles and moxibustion are learned by the official Cang Gong Shenyu." This shows that he understands him. His medical residence has recently moved from the junction of Meibai Road and Ge Road to Heleli, Wuzhen Road, Xinzha Road. I am recording this here for those who suffer from the same diseases.

Travelogue of the South Seas (53)

— Linghua

There are black-headed cranes with red beaks, African black swans, wild cats, Chinese dogs, and several kinds of deer. The spotted deer females have no horns, and the males have horns. By and large, animals without horns tend to be female. This proves the general principle that I have invented that males are sexual and females are not or have less. I have tested the three principles of the French park director: (1) Males and females are generally not in competition; (2) Females compete with females for less; (3) Males compete with males with certainty. The park director deeply agreed. This can prove that today's world wars are just the mutual killing of males. The males agitate and the excuses are material issues and various problems. Do roosters compete only for bread? If it is for food, the mothers bear more responsibility. Why do they not compete? It can be proven that Marx's theory is flawed.

There is a yellow cat as big as a dog, European black rabbits, kangaroos, and white-spotted snakes. The fish is eight feet long and often opens its mouth to release heat. According to the Yuanjian Leihan, the raccoon is good at sleeping and does not wake up, so people say "raccoon sleep." Today, those who say "take a nap" are mistaken. Therefore, those who sleep long and do not wake up are all like raccoons. In the past, the American Elmerson wrote a book called "When Will the Japanese Wake Up?" Looking at this raccoon, I am even more convinced.

The French park director is a strange monk. He is skilled in martial arts, boxing, can write in four styles of calligraphy, and paints. Many people from various places seek his calligraphy. He has been running this park for ten years and has spent over ten thousand. Some people say, "Why does a monk need to do this?" But they do not know that this public figure uses a park as a six realms. A couplet is written on the rockery, saying, "It is good to live here, why not sit for a while? Life is like a dream, advise you not to be too busy." The door plaque says, "Heaven and Man Rejoice." The words "Subduing Dragons and Subduing Tigers" are written on both sides of the rockery. This shows its ambition. However, the South Seas business has not been good in recent years. The daily expenditure is twenty or thirty yuan, and the income is only ten yuan. I heard that in the past, the daily income was fifty yuan. Such academic and cultural institutions should be supported by society and the government. It must be known that the zoo is now the center of learning. Since Lamarck and Darwin, the resolution of social problems has focused on zoology. It sweeps away the fallacies of the era of divine power. Today, my research is based on the physiology of the two sexes and the statistics of war. The root of all evil is the male. It is not really a matter of materialism. It is a great relationship with zoology to explain the origin of sin. Moreover, today's monks are criticized by society for not doing anything. Master Fakong has both literary and martial arts skills and is doing his best for this world's academic achievements. Is he not a strange person in the Buddhist world and a glory of culture? In the park hangs his English medal for competition performance. Another couplet says, "Cranes have dreams of returning to the nest, clouds have no intention of leaving the mountains." You can see his ambition.

That evening, Mr. Dai Shuyuan hosted a banquet and invited reporters from various newspapers. However, few ordinary people have much knowledge of biology, so my three principles are not easy to truly understand.

Warmth in the Heart (280)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Green Bamboo Tears Stain, The Beauty's Heart is Broken; Red Lotus Fragrance Fades, A Maiden's Soul Departs.

The wife became suspicious and recalled all sorts of clues. After that teahouse boy left, she instructed everyone in the household, "When the master comes home, you are not to say anything. You must not tell him that A'tu came." The servants and maids naturally obeyed the wife's orders, because the wife's authority was greater than the master's. Seeing the master being scolded by the wife, they dared not say a word. When the master returned home at twelve o'clock, everyone remained silent. Only the wife spoke, interrogating him like a judge in a court of law. The wife took a puff of her opium pipe and asked, "The ship was late today, wasn't it?" Zhang Yiqing said, "We hadn't even reached Nanjing when we encountered a dense fog. It wouldn't dissipate no matter how hard we tried. Our ship dared not venture into the fog, so we were anchored in the middle of the river for a whole day and night." At this, everyone in the family covered their mouths and chuckled. Even the pipe-lighter, A'bao, dared not give the master a wink, as the wife was watching her very closely. The wife smiled and said, "In that case, you were trapped by the fog." She paused for a moment and said, "Someone told me that they saw you in Shanghai yesterday." Yiqing was taken aback for a moment and quickly defended himself, "How could that be? I was still on the Yangtze River yesterday. Who saw me? Where? That's utter nonsense!" However, although he said this, he was a little flustered, because he had indeed been out yesterday, going to a money exchange on the back street and playing cards at a friend's house in the evening, not returning to his apartment until one o'clock. The wife was truly an excellent judge. She asked her questions calmly and methodically. She took another puff of her pipe and said, "Because the ship you were on arrived yesterday. Someone told me, so I said you returned yesterday." Zhang Yiqing thought, "So it was a sting." He then smiled and said, "I see. But you must know that I didn't return on the same ship. I returned on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangkuan." As a shipping comprador, he was naturally familiar with which ships arrived on which days. At this, the pipe-lighter, A'bao, thought that this was a rather clever answer, but that he shouldn't reveal any more slip-ups. She was like a lawyer accompanying the defendant in court, unable to instruct him on his testimony, yet afraid that he would say something wrong. She was truly on tenterhooks for him. But the interrogator was truly skilled. She said, "Since you took that ship there, why didn't you return on the same ship?" Zhang Yiqing said, "There was a bill to be settled for me at the Hankou office. The manager asked me to stay for a day, so I had no choice but to stay." He thought that this sounded respectable and used the foreign manager to intimidate her, so there was nothing more to say. But he didn't know that he had confirmed to the interrogator that he had taken that ship there. The wife then asked, "That teahouse boy, A'tu, whom I recommended before, isn't he on that ship? Did you see him?" A'bao thought, "If he says he didn't see him, the situation can still be salvaged." But Zhang Yiqing wanted to ingratiate himself with his wife and said, "Yes, I saw him. That person is quite diligent."

Cotton Yarn: The Yarn Market Under the Confrontation of Bulls and Bears

The yarn market fell in the morning and rose in the afternoon. Currently, the bulls and bears are fiercely fighting. Factories are maintaining the 8 tael mark. However, the environment is still not good. Because banditry is rampant everywhere, actual sales are still difficult to prosper. Therefore, the Chaozhou gang is aggressively selling off when prices rise. It can be seen that both sides are competing fiercely. However, actual demand is clearer than yesterday. In the afternoon, the gold industry purchased and Ruida was mostly short, and the market atmosphere suddenly became tight. Therefore, prices rose by one tael for each month. The overall situation may stabilize. The future depends on demand for a turnaround.

Man-Made Standard Cotton Fell in the Morning and Rose in the Afternoon: The man-made standard cotton market opened with American cotton flat and weak. The market situation was still not good. The selling atmosphere was strong, and prices fell by two or three qian. The trend continued to fall for two or three rounds, resulting in falls of seven, eight, and nine qian. In the afternoon, the market rose sharply, and the situation became tense. It was said that there was news of peace, so retail investors echoed the purchase, and prices rose by 1 tael and 3 qian for each month. Total transactions for the day were 19,550 bales. Sen Kang sold 1,000 bales, Dafeng 1,200 bales, Gongtai 800 bales, Yichang 650 bales, Tianlong 900 bales, and the others 200 bales to 550 bales. Ruida bought 1,600 bales, Yiyu 1,450 bales, Hanyue 900 bales, Tianjiang 900 bales, Meiji 700 bales, and the others 350 bales to 800 bales. The closing price of man-made standard cotton is recorded on the left.

Cotton Sales Active, Market Stable

The cotton market was weak in the morning and strong in the afternoon. The situation in the American cotton market was still flat. The easing of foreign exchange rates made the combined price of foreign cotton cheaper. Therefore, Shenxin Factory purchased 6,000 bales of Lumi Special American cotton at a price of 37 taels and 5 qian to 8 taels and 11 months for delivery to the factory. The Han gang sold off at rising prices. The cotton market should tend to be stable. However, the inland gangs, due to the poor harvest, purchased but did not sell and had a strong bullish mentality. In addition, leather factories, due to cotton yarn relations, purchased standard cotton at a limited price of 2 taels for the 11th and 12th months. Therefore, morale was slightly stable. Actual sales in the factory were slightly traded. However, Japanese factories remained quietly unmoved.

Han Cotton Rose After Falling: The Han cotton market opened with American cotton flat. The weather was clear, and retail investors sold off, and the market fell steadily. Prices fell by 1 qian and 5 fen for each month. In the afternoon, the yarn market rose sharply, and the cotton market led the rise by 1 qian and 5 fen to 2 qian. Total transactions for the day were 46,200 dan. Daji sold 3,300 dan, Yicheng 2,500 dan, Dafeng 1,600 dan, Maoji 1,400 dan, and the rest 1,100 to 1,200 dan. Changji bought 1,100 dan, Gongtai 3,900 dan, Hanfeng 1,500 dan, Ruida 2,500 dan, Tianchang 1,600 dan, Xiesheng 2,300 dan, and the rest 900 to 1,200 dan. Grain: The Jing Rice Market in Hexia is Stable and the Xian Rice Market is Weak

Zhabei: Yesterday, ships from Luli came, and the remaining numbers sold well. High-quality broken Jing rice was still in short supply. Zhongguan had a slight large-volume sale, and all were finalized. Ordinary was still at 20 yuan and 7 or 8 jiao. Xixin Jing rice was increasingly scarce, and the market remained at 20 yuan and 5 jiao. Dongxin Jing rice was also still at 20 yuan. Xinyang Xian rice was weak as the weather turned clear and people tended to soften, and prices fell by 3 or 4 jiao. It must be especially high to open at 15 yuan, 2 or 3 jiao, and ordinary was about 15 yuan. Xin Kejian also fell by 2 or 3 jiao. Carloads arrived at the port and were sold one after another. The market was not prosperous, and the price was 14 yuan, 2 or 3 jiao. Medium quality was 13 yuan and a half. All the tips were declining, but Duzi Xian was priced at 16 yuan and a half to 17 yuan because of the shortage. The market for changed yuan was weak, and there were no gains or losses.

Hunan, Shanghai: There were only a few sources from Hexia. There was still no high-quality white broken rice. Ordinary goods in the market were also extremely scarce. Prices were stable. Xinjing was increasingly scarce, and the market still followed Zhabei and changed. Qingpu and other Xinxiang Jing were still at 20 yuan and a half. Xin Jian was slightly arriving at the port. Yangdu Jian also felt sluggish. Sales in the market were flat due to the clear weather. Prices were slightly different by 2 or 3 jiao. Baiyuan followed, and shipments were sold as they arrived. Luli production messages were still tight, so this cargo was still opened high at 19 yuan to 18 yuan, 7 or 8 jiao.

The Flour Market is Weak and Lifeless

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, prices mostly tended to stabilize. Due to the slight fluctuations in foreign wheat quotations, short positions outside the industry were replenished with the market. Therefore, it seemed that the market had turned stable, but the environment felt secretly weak. After the market opened in the afternoon, near-term and long-term periods felt stable and sluggish. The main cause of the turbulence was the heavy decline in the city. The external exchange rate was gradually extended, as if to give a good and cost-effective order for foreign wheat. Therefore, large and small factories that had already started ordering foreign wheat also sold off one after another, causing people's hearts to be greatly weakened. There was a fall in the fourth customs level from November onwards. This situation was completely driven by foreign countries, and it is still uncertain whether it is optimistic that the exchange rate will lengthen later. As a result, this month fell 1.5 points compared to the previous day, October fell 1 point and 7 li and a half, November and December fell 1.5 points, January fell 2 points, and February fell 1.5 points.

The Wheat Market is Still Difficult to Advance

Another Wave of Selling... The Flour Market Reports a Fall

Yesterday, after the period wheat market opened in the morning, the market in each month tended to be stable. There was a situation where short positions were slightly offset due to the seemingly flat situation, and the market relied on it to hold. When it opened in the afternoon, a small factory was already short, and due to the lengthening of the exchange rate, another batch was sold off, and the fall in the flour market caused each month to be unstable. If the exchange rate changes again, the future is still looking small. As a result, this month fell 0.3 points compared to the previous day, October fell 1 point, November fell 0.3 points, December and January fell 1.2 points, and February fell 0.3 points. Each factory in the spot wheat market once again rejected each other, and the firm rejection of this type of factory seemed to be an opportunity. A total of 2,000 packages of Shandong, Yaowan, and Shashi wheat were opened in the city. The price was slightly lower than the previous day by 2 or 3 points, and Fuxin reluctantly ate it.

Silk and Tea: Wuxi Autumn Cocoon Production is Poor and of Poor Quality

Only 20 to 30% Harvest... Drying Loss Requires 400 Jin

This year, the farmers in Wuxi townships were not weak in their autumn silkworm breeding, thanks to the promotion by government offices and silk merchants. However, before and after the big sleep, the weather suddenly changed, and the autumn rain did not stop. In addition, the weather was severe, resulting in the outbreak of silkworm diseases and extremely poor harvests. The total harvest was only 20 to 30%. Although a small number of scales were opened in various cocoon banks, the quality of the cocoons was exceptionally poor, and the drying loss required 400 jin.

Zhabei

Yesterday, seventeen or eighteen boats arrived from the river below. Eastern new japonica rice and old thin paddy rice were scarce and priced high. Northern help broken japonica rice was lacking and not opened. The remaining prices were stable, only the new port tip, water chestnut tip, new Dujian, and new yang tip of medium and lower quality were slightly more expensive.

Shanghai Market

Market News

Wan Yuan Xiang Embroidery Shop, located at the west end of Huajin Lane on Sanma Road, declares that this shop has devoted great effort to researching embroidery techniques. All drafts are meticulously created by famous calligraphers and painters. Hundreds of female workers in the Xiangzhong factory are well-trained. The embroidery work is quite capable of maintaining the original color of the draft. Recently, due to the raging red atmosphere in Changsha, a large number of embroidered goods have been shipped to Shanghai. Fine products abound, allowing people to choose and purchase, which is a great opportunity for happy birthdays and gift-giving. Please do not miss it.

Da Sheng Trading Company, located at No. 7 Ningbo Road, Shanghai, declares that the Xu's rotary mimeograph produced by the Zhengyuan Industrial Cooperative, managed by this company, has been widely praised and admired by all walks of life. The printing is convenient. The machine is made entirely of metal, so it is extremely sturdy and durable. The action is sensitive and the printing is clear. It can also print two or three colors or more at the same time. The price is lower than foreign goods, and the value is only 100 yuan. Various institutions, organizations, schools, and firms in this city and other places have adopted this machine, so buyers are extremely enthusiastic. In addition, this company has detailed instructions. A letter with four cents postage attached will be sent.

China Investment Company, located at No. 38 Avenue Edward VII, declares that this company is engaged in real estate construction business in this city. Now, in view of the fact that Shanghai is a place where people from all walks of life gather, both good and bad, and that the issue of housing is very important to citizens, it has specially established a real estate rental department to promote social progress and improve the lives of the people. All citizens who want to rent a house and want to have good neighbors, and landlords who want to find good tenants can be introduced. It is now heard that there are a large number of clients entrusting both parties, and in the future, benefiting the society is not a small matter.

Yuxing Biscuit Company declares that this company has specially hired technicians who have studied in Europe and have rich experience to carefully produce various Western-style biscuits. They are crisp and delicious, and are very different from the ordinary biscuits used in the market. The taste is sweet without being greasy, and the quality is light without harming the spleen and stomach. Therefore, Western countries have tried to cater to the tastes of the Chinese people and have competed to sell and ship, stealing my money. Although this is a small matter, the outflow of rights and interests is as numerous as the sands of the Ganges. Recently, Chinese people have become more aware and have set up factories to manufacture to meet domestic demand. However, Chinese people only know how to imitate without adding research. No wonder they are inferior to foreign goods. This company, in view of this, has exhausted several years of effort to refer to the mysteries of this field and obtained its good method. It has specially made various Western-style biscuits. Its products are not only different from ordinary biscuits, but also surpass imported products. The price is particularly low. All patriotic gentlemen can come and get them. The address is No. 140 Avenue Joffre, French Concession.

Rui Yuan Xiang Silk and Cloth Shop, located across from Zhejiang Road and Xiamen Road, declares that this shop will hold a grand sale and give away gifts for 28 days to celebrate the tenth anniversary of its founding on the 19th day of the ninth month of the national calendar. In addition, a discount department will be set up in this shop to implement a "buy one foot, get one yard free" policy to repay the elegant intentions of its patrons. The rest of the newly arrived goods have fresh and abundant patterns, and the prices are unusually cheap. Don't miss the good opportunity, don't miss it.

Theater News

Paris Grand Theater declares that this theater will from today screen Niao Fa Company's latest great production of 1930, "Desire Sea Love Sky". The film is starring Europe's most beautiful female star, Betty Amann, and the conflict between flesh and spirit, the male lead, Florelle, is a sad and gorgeous film that has shocked the world. The crazy and unrestrained parts are intoxicating and bone-eroding, the sad parts make people linger and want to cry, and the ending's sweet entanglement is very thought-provoking. Recently, it was simultaneously screened in various Shochiku theaters in Tokyo, Osaka, Kobe, Japan, and lasted for a month.

Nanjing Road Flower World declares that since the opening of this world, all the performances have been excellent, so the tourists are quite crowded. The manager of this venue, Cheng Xiqing, and the assistant manager, Wang Keyang, in order to arouse the interest of tourists, specially ordered Da Yi Ban to rehearse this play, and instructed Xiaofeng Society to compile and perform a new play of current affairs, "The Death of the Actress". They are currently rushing to prepare the costumes and scenery, etc., and will be able to start performing soon. It is also scheduled that starting this Friday, the 19th, tickets will be sold for one dime to show preferential treatment to customers.

Five Star Film Company declares that the company's first production, "Lone Mountain Flying Hero", was originally scheduled to start filming on the 18th. Now, in order to take it seriously, Chen Kai and Yu Xia, who have film experience, will jointly direct. The brave male lead will be played by Chen Kai himself. The female lead has hired Xu Suzhen.

Publishing News

The United Bookstore on Fourth Horse Road declares that the books published by this store on journalism are all famous works at home and abroad, and are not only suitable as textbooks for journalism departments in universities, but also must-reads for those engaged in journalism and scholars who study journalism. For example, the newly published "History of Chinese Journalism" is a meticulous work by Huang Tianpeng, praised by the Japanese as a representative work of the Chinese journalism circle. It has been adopted as a textbook by the Journalism Department of Fudan University and the Journalism Department of Yenching University. Another example is "Collection of Famous Essays on Journalism", which was originally designated as a reference book by various schools. Due to the poor content of the first edition, it has been re-selected and revised to a 25-format book, and the price is still sold for one yuan. Another example is "Business Management of Journalism", which is Mr. Wu Dingjiu's lecture at Peking University, which focuses on practice and does not make empty talk. "An Outline of Journalism" is a masterpiece by the Japanese Chu Ren Guan, which analyzes journalism in great detail. In addition, "An Outline of Journalism" by Xu Shihuang, a senior journalist, will also be published by this store and will be available early next month.
